Use `gemini-2.0-flash-exp` (fastest model)\\n2. Reduce function execution time\\n3. Check network latency\\n4. Consider local caching\\n\\n### Function Call Failures\\n\\nCommon issues:\\n- Parameter type mismatches → Check FunctionTool parameters\\n- Missing required params → Ensure all required params specified\\n- Function errors → Add try/catch to function implementations\\n\\n## 🤝 Contributing\\n\\nContributions welcome! Areas for improvement:\\n- Additional watermarking schemes\\n- Advanced semantic memory (vector DB integration)\\n- More JR validation strategies\\n- Performance optimizations\\n\\n## 📄 License\\n\\nMIT License - Free to use and modify\\n\\n## 🙏 Acknowledgments\\n\\n- Google Gemini Team for native function calling\\n- AutoGen for inspiration and baseline comparison\\n- PNKLN community for architecture guidance\\n\\n---\\n\\n**Built with ❤️ for the PNKLN Core Stack**\\n\\n**Questions?** Open an issue or check the examples!\\n=======\\n# Gemini Ingestion Layer - PNKLN Core Stack™\\n\\nIntelligent data collection and classification pipeline for the PNKLN Core Stack™. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│                                                             │\\n│  ┌────────────┐  ┌────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐          │\\n│  │  YouTube   │  │  Twitter   │  │    News     │          │\\n│  │ Collector  │  │ Collector  │  │  Collector  │          │\\n│  └─────┬──────┘  └─────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘          │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│  ┌─────┴───────┬────────┴────────┬────────┴──────┐         │\\n│  │    RSS      │  Web Scraper    │ API Integrator│         │\\n│  │  Collector  │                 │               │         │\\n│  └─────┬───────┴────────┬────────┴────────┬──────┘         │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│        └────────────────┼─────────────────┘                 │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Tier Classification │                        │\\n│              │   (Tier 1/2/3)      │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Ethical Compliance  │                        │\\n│              │    Validation       │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1. Areas for improvement:\\n- Additional watermarking schemes\\n- Advanced semantic memory (vector DB integration)\\n- More JR validation strategies\\n- Performance optimizations\\n\\n## 📄 License\\n\\nMIT License - Free to use and modify\\n\\n## 🙏 Acknowledgments\\n\\n- Google Gemini Team for native function calling\\n- AutoGen for inspiration and baseline comparison\\n- PNKLN community for architecture guidance\\n\\n---\\n\\n**Built with ❤️ for the PNKLN Core Stack**\\n\\n**Questions?** Open an issue or check the examples!\\n=======\\n# Gemini Ingestion Layer - PNKLN Core Stack™\\n\\nIntelligent data collection and classification pipeline for the PNKLN Core Stack™. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│                                                             │\\n│  ┌────────────┐  ┌────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐          │\\n│  │  YouTube   │  │  Twitter   │  │    News     │          │\\n│  │ Collector  │  │ Collector  │  │  Collector  │          │\\n│  └─────┬──────┘  └─────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘          │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│  ┌─────┴───────┬────────┴────────┬────────┴──────┐         │\\n│  │    RSS      │  Web Scraper    │ API Integrator│         │\\n│  │  Collector  │                 │               │         │\\n│  └─────┬───────┴────────┬────────┴────────┬──────┘         │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│        └────────────────┼─────────────────┘                 │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Tier Classification │                        │\\n│              │   (Tier 1/2/3)      │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Ethical Compliance  │                        │\\n│              │    Validation       │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1. Areas for improvement:\\n- Additional watermarking schemes\\n- Advanced semantic memory (vector DB integration)\\n- More JR validation strategies\\n- Performance optimizations\\n\\n## 📄 License\\n\\nMIT License - Free to use and modify\\n\\n## 🙏 Acknowledgments\\n\\n- Google Gemini Team for native function calling\\n- AutoGen for inspiration and baseline comparison\\n- PNKLN community for architecture guidance\\n\\n---\\n\\n**Built with ❤️ for the PNKLN Core Stack**\\n\\n**Questions?** Open an issue or check the examples!\\n=======\\n# Gemini Ingestion Layer - PNKLN Core Stack™\\n\\nIntelligent data collection and classification pipeline for the PNKLN Core Stack™. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│                                                             │\\n│  ┌────────────┐  ┌────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐          │\\n│  │  YouTube   │  │  Twitter   │  │    News     │          │\\n│  │ Collector  │  │ Collector  │  │  Collector  │          │\\n│  └─────┬──────┘  └─────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘          │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│  ┌─────┴───────┬────────┴────────┬────────┴──────┐         │\\n│  │    RSS      │  Web Scraper    │ API Integrator│         │\\n│  │  Collector  │                 │               │         │\\n│  └─────┬───────┴────────┬────────┴────────┬──────┘         │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│        └────────────────┼─────────────────┘                 │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Tier Classification │                        │\\n│              │   (Tier 1/2/3)      │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Ethical Compliance  │                        │\\n│              │    Validation       │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│ Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1. Areas for improvement:\\n- Additional watermarking schemes\\n- Advanced semantic memory (vector DB integration)\\n- More JR validation strategies\\n- Performance optimizations\\n\\n## 📄 License\\n\\nMIT License - Free to use and modify\\n\\n## 🙏 Acknowledgments\\n\\n- Google Gemini Team for native function calling\\n- AutoGen for inspiration and baseline comparison\\n- PNKLN community for architecture guidance\\n\\n---\\n\\n**Built with ❤️ for the PNKLN Core Stack**\\n\\n**Questions?** Open an issue or check the examples!\\n=======\\n# Gemini Ingestion Layer - PNKLN Core Stack™\\n\\nIntelligent data collection and classification pipeline for the PNKLN Core Stack™. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│                                                             │\\n│  ┌────────────┐  ┌────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐          │\\n│  │  YouTube   │  │  Twitter   │  │    News     │          │\\n│  │ Collector  │  │ Collector  │  │  Collector  │          │\\n│  └─────┬──────┘  └─────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘          │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│  ┌─────┴───────┬────────┴────────┬────────┴──────┐         │\\n│  │    RSS      │  Web Scraper    │ API Integrator│         │\\n│  │  Collector  │                 │               │         │\\n│  └─────┬───────┴────────┬────────┴────────┬──────┘         │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│        └────────────────┼─────────────────┘                 │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Tier Classification │                        │\\n│              │   (Tier 1/2/3)      │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Ethical Compliance  │                        │\\n│              │    Validation       │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1. Use `gemini-2.0-flash-exp` (fastest model)\\n2. Reduce function execution time\\n3. Check network latency\\n4. Consider local caching\\n\\n### Function Call Failures\\n\\nCommon issues:\\n- Parameter type mismatches → Check FunctionTool parameters\\n- Missing required params → Ensure all required params specified\\n- Function errors → Add try/catch to function implementations\\n\\n## 🤝 Contributing\\n\\nContributions welcome! Areas for improvement:\\n- Additional watermarking schemes\\n- Advanced semantic memory (vector DB integration)\\n- More JR validation strategies\\n- Performance optimizations\\n\\n## 📄 License\\n\\nMIT License - Free to use and modify\\n\\n## 🙏 Acknowledgments\\n\\n- Google Gemini Team for native function calling\\n- AutoGen for inspiration and baseline comparison\\n- PNKLN community for architecture guidance\\n\\n---\\n\\n**Built with ❤️ for the PNKLN Core Stack**\\n\\n**Questions?** Open an issue or check the examples!\\n=======\\n# Gemini Ingestion Layer - PNKLN Core Stack™\\n\\nIntelligent data collection and classification pipeline for the PNKLN Core Stack™. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│                                                             │\\n│  ┌────────────┐  ┌────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐          │\\n│  │  YouTube   │  │  Twitter   │  │    News     │          │\\n│  │ Collector  │  │ Collector  │  │  Collector  │          │\\n│  └─────┬──────┘  └─────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘          │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│  ┌─────┴───────┬────────┴────────┬────────┴──────┐         │\\n│  │    RSS      │  Web Scraper    │ API Integrator│         │\\n│  │  Collector  │                 │               │         │\\n│  └─────┬───────┴────────┬────────┴────────┬──────┘         │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│        └────────────────┼─────────────────┘                 │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Tier Classification │                        │\\n│              │   (Tier 1/2/3)      │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Ethical Compliance  │                        │\\n│              │    Validation       │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1. Areas for improvement:\\n- Additional watermarking schemes\\n- Advanced semantic memory (vector DB integration)\\n- More JR validation strategies\\n- Performance optimizations\\n\\n## 📄 License\\n\\nMIT License - Free to use and modify\\n\\n## 🙏 Acknowledgments\\n\\n- Google Gemini Team for native function calling\\n- AutoGen for inspiration and baseline comparison\\n- PNKLN community for architecture guidance\\n\\n---\\n\\n**Built with ❤️ for the PNKLN Core Stack**\\n\\n**Questions?** Open an issue or check the examples!\\n=======\\n# Gemini Ingestion Layer - PNKLN Core Stack™\\n\\nIntelligent data collection and classification pipeline for the PNKLN Core Stack™. This service operates as a GKE CronJob that gathers intelligence from multiple sources nightly, classifies items by tier, and makes data available for downstream processing.\\n\\n## Overview\\n\\nThe Gemini Ingestion Layer is a foundational component that:\\n- Collects data from 6+ sources (YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web, APIs)\\n- Classifies items into 3 tiers based on authority, relevance, and timeliness\\n- Ensures ethical crawling compliance (robots.txt, rate limiting)\\n- Delivers processed intelligence to Judge 6 and AM Briefing services\\n- Operates within a ~$77/month budget at ~45 minutes runtime per night\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\n```\\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\\n│              Gemini Ingestion Layer (GKE)                   │\\n│                                                             │\\n│  ┌────────────┐  ┌────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐          │\\n│  │  YouTube   │  │  Twitter   │  │    News     │          │\\n│  │ Collector  │  │ Collector  │  │  Collector  │          │\\n│  └─────┬──────┘  └─────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘          │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│  ┌─────┴───────┬────────┴────────┬────────┴──────┐         │\\n│  │    RSS      │  Web Scraper    │ API Integrator│         │\\n│  │  Collector  │                 │               │         │\\n│  └─────┬───────┴────────┬────────┴────────┬──────┘         │\\n│        │                │                 │                 │\\n│        └────────────────┼─────────────────┘                 │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Tier Classification │                        │\\n│              │   (Tier 1/2/3)      │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │ Ethical Compliance  │                        │\\n│              │    Validation       │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Quality Scoring    │                        │\\n│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │\\n│                         │                                   │\\n│              ┌──────────▼──────────┐                        │\\n│              │  Storage (GCS/DB)   │                        │\\n│              └─────────────────────┘                        │\\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\\n```\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n- **Multi-Source Collection**: YouTube, Twitter, News, RSS, Web scraping, API integrations\\n- **Intelligent Tier Classification**: ML-based classification (Tier 1/2/3)\\n- **Ethical Crawling**: 100% robots.txt compliance, adaptive rate limiting\\n- **Cost Efficient**: ~$77/month operational cost (~$0.012 per item)\\n- **FastAPI Integration**: REST API for triggering, querying, and monitoring\\n- **GKE Native**: Kubernetes CronJob with multi-container orchestration\\n- **Quality Gated**: Relevance, completeness, and timeliness checks\\n\\n## Quick Start\\n\\n### Prerequisites\\n\\n- Python 3.11+\\n- Google Cloud Platform account\\n- GKE cluster\\n- PostgreSQL database\\n- Redis instance\\n\\n### Installation\\n\\n1. **Clone the repository**:\\n   ```bash\\n   git clone https://github.com/ehanc69/ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services.git\\n   cd ShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Install Python dependencies**:\\n   ```bash\\n   pip install -r requirements.txt\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Configure environment**:\\n   ```bash\\n   cp .env.example .env\\n   # Edit .env with your credentials\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Deploy to GKE**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n### Running Locally\\n\\n**Start the FastAPI server**:\\n```bash\\nuvicorn src.api.ingestion:app --reload --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\\n```\\n\\n**Access the API**:\\n- Swagger UI: http://localhost:8000/docs\\n- ReDoc: http://localhost:8000/redoc\\n\\n## API Endpoints\\n\\n### Core Endpoints\\n\\n| Method | Endpoint | Description |\\n|--------|----------|-------------|\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/trigger` | Manually trigger ingestion job |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/status` | Get job status (current or by ID) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/items` | Query ingested items (with filters) |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/metrics` | Performance metrics |\\n| `GET` | `/ingestion/sources` | Get source configuration |\\n| `POST` | `/ingestion/sources` | Update source configuration |\\n\\n### Example Usage\\n\\n**Trigger manual ingestion**:\\n```bash\\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:8000/ingestion/trigger \\\\\\n  -H \\\"Content-Type: application/json\\\" \\\\\\n  -d '{\\\"reason\\\": \\\"Breaking news event\\\", \\\"override_schedule\\\": true}'\\n```\\n\\n**Query Tier 1 items**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/items?tier=tier_1&limit=10\\\"\\n```\\n\\n**Get metrics**:\\n```bash\\ncurl \\\"http://localhost:8000/ingestion/metrics?days=7\\\"\\n```\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\n### Source Configuration\\n\\nEdit `config/sources.yaml` to add/modify data sources:\\n\\n```yaml\\nsources:\\n  - type: youtube\\n    enabled: true\\n    channels:\\n      - UCxxxxxxxx\\n    max_videos_per_channel: 50\\n\\n  - type: twitter\\n    enabled: true\\n    keywords:\\n      - \\\"AI\\\"\\n      - \\\"machine learning\\\"\\n```\\n\\n### Tier Classification\\n\\nEdit `config/tier-classification.yaml` to adjust tier rules:\\n\\n```yaml\\ntier_1:\\n  min_authority: 90\\n  max_age_hours: 6\\n  min_relevance: 80\\n  min_engagement: 1000\\n```\\n\\n### Ethical Crawling\\n\\nEdit `config/ethical-crawling.yaml` to configure compliance:\\n\\n```yaml\\nrate_limiting:\\n  default_delay_seconds: 2\\n  adaptive: true\\n\\nrobots_txt:\\n  enabled: true\\n  respect_crawl_delay: true\\n```\\n\\n## Performance Metrics\\n\\n### Target SLAs\\n\\n| Metric | Target |\\n|--------|--------|\\n| Runtime | ≤45 minutes |\\n| Daily Items | 1000-5000 |\\n| Active Sources | ≥6 |\\n| Cost/Item | ≤$0.015 |\\n| Relevance (Avg) | ≥60/100 |\\n| Tier 1 % | 10-20% |\\n| Uptime | ≥99% |\\n\\n### Current Performance\\n\\nSee the [Gemini Ingestion Layer Analysis](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md) for detailed performance analysis.\\n\\n## Tier Definitions\\n\\n### Tier 1 (Priority Intelligence)\\n- High-authority sources (verified news, official channels)\\n- Time-critical (≤6 hours old)\\n- High relevance (≥80/100)\\n- Strong engagement (≥1000 signals)\\n- **Target**: 10-20% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 2 (Standard Intelligence)\\n- Moderate-authority sources\\n- Standard timeliness (≤72 hours)\\n- Moderate relevance (≥50/100)\\n- Moderate engagement (100-1000)\\n- **Target**: 30-40% of total items\\n\\n### Tier 3 (Background Intelligence)\\n- Lower-authority sources\\n- Older content (>72 hours)\\n- Tangential relevance (<50/100)\\n- Low engagement (<100)\\n- **Target**: 40-60% of total items\\n\\n## Ethical Guidelines\\n\\nWe adhere to strict ethical standards:\\n\\n- ✅ **100% robots.txt compliance**: Never violate crawler policies\\n- ✅ **Adaptive rate limiting**: Prevent server overload\\n- ✅ **Transparent identification**: Clear User-Agent with contact info\\n- ✅ **No paywall circumvention**: Respect premium content\\n- ✅ **PII scrubbing**: Remove personal information\\n- ✅ **GDPR compliant**: Right to erasure, data retention limits\\n\\nSee [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md) for details.\\n\\n## Development\\n\\n### Project Structure\\n\\n```\\nShadowTag-v2-fastapi-services/\\n├── docs/\\n│   ├── architecture/          # Architecture documentation\\n│   │   ├── gemini-ingestion-layer.md\\n│   │   ├── ethical-crawling.md\\n│   │   └── tier-classification.md\\n│   └── prompts/               # Analysis prompts\\n│       └── gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md\\n├── src/\\n│   ├── api/                   # FastAPI endpoints\\n│   │   └── ingestion.py\\n│   ├── collectors/            # Source-specific collectors\\n│   ├── processors/            # Tier classification, quality scoring\\n│   └── utils/                 # Shared utilities\\n├── config/                    # Configuration files\\n│   ├── ethical-crawling.yaml\\n│   ├── tier-classification.yaml\\n│   ├── sources.yaml\\n│   └── quality-gates.yaml\\n├── k8s/                       # Kubernetes manifests\\n│   └── ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n├── models/                    # ML models\\n├── data/                      # Data files\\n├── schemas/                   # JSON schemas\\n├── requirements.txt           # Python dependencies\\n├── package.json               # Node.js dependencies\\n└── README.md\\n```\\n\\n### Running Tests\\n\\n```bash\\npytest tests/ --cov=src --cov-report=html\\n```\\n\\n### Code Quality\\n\\n```bash\\n# Format code\\nblack src/\\nisort src/\\n\\n# Lint\\nflake8 src/\\nmypy src/\\n```\\n\\n## Deployment\\n\\n### GKE Deployment\\n\\n1. **Create namespace**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **Configure secrets**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl create secret generic ingestion-secrets \\\\\\n     --from-literal=youtube_api_key=YOUR_KEY \\\\\\n     --from-literal=twitter_bearer_token=YOUR_TOKEN \\\\\\n     --namespace pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n3. **Deploy CronJob**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl apply -f k8s/ingestion-cronjob.yaml\\n   ```\\n\\n4. **Monitor**:\\n   ```bash\\n   kubectl get cronjobs -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   kubectl logs -f job/gemini-ingestion-layer-XXXXX -n pnkln-ingestion\\n   ```\\n\\n## Monitoring & Alerting\\n\\n### Prometheus Metrics\\n\\n- `ingestion_items_total{tier}`: Total items by tier\\n- `ingestion_runtime_seconds`: Job runtime\\n- `ingestion_cost_usd`: Operational cost\\n- `ingestion_relevance_score`: Average relevance\\n- `ingestion_errors_total{source}`: Errors by source\\n\\n### Grafana Dashboards\\n\\nImport dashboards from `dashboards/` directory:\\n- Tier Distribution Over Time\\n- Source Performance\\n- Cost Tracking\\n- Quality Metrics\\n\\n## Migration from Claude Code SDK\\n\\nThis project has been migrated from `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` to `@anthropic-ai/claude-agent-sdk`. See [MIGRATION.md](MIGRATION.md) for details.\\n\\n## Documentation\\n\\n- [Architecture Overview](docs/architecture/gemini-ingestion-layer.md)\\n- [Ethical Crawling Guidelines](docs/architecture/ethical-crawling.md)\\n- [Tier Classification Model](docs/architecture/tier-classification.md)\\n- [Analysis Prompt](docs/prompts/gemini-ingestion-layer-analysis.md)\\n\\n## Contributing\\n\\n1.
